72.1(1): dbyings: rtogs grol sangs rgyas kun gyi mchog: bde chen kun bzang klong du

72.5(1): med nam mkha'i rang bzhin te: sems nyid nam mkha' bon nyid gsum: mi 'byed

72.10(1): nyid la: 'pho 'gyur dri ma med pa'i phyir: sems nyid thig le nyag gcig la: 'pho

72.13(1): pa'i phyir: sems nyid thig le nyag gcig la: mtshan ma med pas rang 'byung

72.18(1): nam mkha' bon nyid la: g.yo rtsol dri ma med pa'i phyir: sems nyid thig le nyag

73.1(1): rang 'byung bde'o: nam mkha' rtag chad med pa'i phyir: bon nyid dbyings la rtag

73.3(1): nyid thig le nyag gcig la: rtag chad med pa'i rang 'byung bde'o: nam mkha' 
73.4(1): mtshon du med pa'i phyir: bon nyid dbyings la mtshon du med: de ltar nam mkha'

73.19(1): med pas mu med bdal: gza' gtad med pas mtha' bral don: tha snyad med 
73.20(1): pas gang mi 'dzin: de bzhin gnas lugs snying po'i don: ye nas nam mkha'i rang 
73.21(1): bzhin te: snang 'jug mtha' dang bral ba ru: rtsol bas las kyis rkyen mi ldang :
74.1(1): rtog pa blo 'byung smrig sgyu la: rgyu ba'i bag chags rjes mi 'dzin: glo bur yid kyi cho

74.12(1): kun tu bzang po rang 'byung spungs so hrun: e ma khyab bdal rdzogs pa chen po'i 
74.13(1): don: rang bzhin lhun grub bon nyid klong yangs mdzod: rig pa'i rgyal po snang 
74.14(1): srid kun 'byung gter: shes bya gcig rdzogs yon tan thabs kyi mchog: gang gis 
74.15(1): mi bsgribs phyi nang zangs thal sgron: snang srid kun gsal ci snyed mnyam pa'i spyan:
74.16(1): skye 'gul cho 'phrul ma lus 'byung ba'i gzhi: yod med bsrid pa gang gis skyed pa'i
